Our vision involves expanding from hundreds of personalized treatments today to potentially thousands, powered by richer insights from lab diagnostics, growing subscriber data sets, and eventually daily tracking from wearable devices. This will unlock faster feedback loops and interventions resulting in greater optimized care. Next, we will continue expanding into new specialties that deeply impact people's lives.
